 1
 Keep the right place of things in the right way - First of all, separate the waste items in the kitchen

 4

 " World Hearing Day 2019: It is said that if music is heard in free time, then the person becomes relieved
 is baat ko follow karte hue ham log din main najaane kitne ghante yearphone par gane sunne main vyateet kar dete hai
 There is nothing wrong with listening to songs, but the earphones you use affect your hearing
 aaj world hearing de par aapako bataate hai yearphone ke nakaaratmak prabhaavon ke bare main or jaanate hai is samasya se kaise bachaa saktaa he
 This time, the theme of World Hearing Day is 'check your hearing'
 bataa den, vishwa swasth sanghathan ke anusaar puri duniya main 466 million log aise hai, jinhone apni sunne kii kshamta kho di he or bhavishya main ye aankada 630 million ke paar ja saktaa he
 It is being said that the increasing inclination of people towards earphones is making this problem more serious
 aaj world hearing de par vishwa swasthya sanghathan (WHO) ne ek nai ap 'hearwho' shuru kii he
 This app can be run on ios and Android
 or play store par uplabdh he
 This app will assess the hearing ability of your ears
 aapako bas yearphone lagaana he or ye test karnaa he
 After this you will be given a score, which will show how good your hearing is
 agar aapkaa score kam aata he to ye ap aapako kisi ianti doctor ko dikhaane kii salaah bhi detii he
 By the way, many people in India have difficulty hearing, but doctors say that this problem can be fixed
 vaise ab OAE or BERA jaise test uplabdh hai, jinase bina dard ke kaanon kii samaysya ke bare main pataa chal saktaa he or aap thik samay par iskaa ilaaj karvaa sakate hai
 You can fall prey to these problems by using earphones more
 air paisej band hone kaa khatra- aaj kal ke nae yearphone aisi technology ke saath aa rahe hai ki aap bahut badhiya aawaaj main sab kuch sun sakate hai
 But reading these earphones you have to place near your ear canal, due to which the air flow stops in the ears
 iske chalate aap kaaphi tip ke kaan ke infections se grast ho sakate hai
 2
 kaanon kaa sunn hona- jo log din main kai ghante yearphone prayog karte hai, unhen ye anubhav jarur hua hoga
 When we keep the earphones on for a long time and then remove them, it makes our ears numb
 hamen thode samay ke liye kuch bhi saaf sunai nahin detaa
 Initially this problem seems small but in the long run it can affect your hearing ability forever
 3
 Negative effect on the brain- If you are using too much earphones, it can have negative effects on your brain too
 yearphone se electromagnetic vevs nikalati hai, jo lambey samay ke liye hamaare dimag kii functioning par bhi asar daal sakati hai
 Let us know, the inner part of our ear is attached to the brain, so if there will be any problem in the ear, then it can also have an effect on our brain

 Three yogas are considered the most auspicious in astrology
 agar aapkikundli main ye mahayogho to aap bhi iskaa laabh uthaa sakate hai bas aapako kuch baton kaa dhyaan rakhana hoga
 Let us know what these three grand totals are
 
 
 gajakesari yoga- jyotish kaa sabase bada or sabase zyada shubh yoga manaa jaataa he
 - When this yoga is in the horoscope, the person becomes special
 - jab chandramaa se brihaspati centre main ho tab is yoga kaa nirmaan hota he
 In this yoga, if Jupiter is in Cancer or Moon is in Taurus, then a person makes history
 - is yoga kii mahatvapurn baat yah he ki chandramaa yaa brihaspati ast na hon na hi papakrant hon, tabhi iskaa fal mil paayegaa
 - In Jupiter head lagna this yoga is more effective
 agar kundali main gajakesari yoga ho to kin baton kaa khyaal rakhen-- jin kundaliyon main yah yoga ho aise logon ko apane bade bujurgon, mata-pita kaa sammaan jarur karnaa chahie
 - Such people should keep sattvikta in their food and behavior
 - jhooth bolne se or maance-madiraa prayog karne se parhez karnaa chahie
 - Both worship Vela God
 budhaditya yoga- yah sabase zyada kundaliyon main paaya jane vaala yoga he, or is yoga kii prabalata bahut zyada hoti he
 - It is formed by the presence of Sun and Mercury together- On this yoga, one gets respect and wealth and the person is very powerful
 - yah yoga tabhi falit hota he jab yah centre athwa trikon main bana ho tathaa budh ast na hedgar kundali main budhaditya yoga ho to kis prakaar laabh uthaayen- suryoday ke purv uthne kaa prayaas karnaa chahie
 - One should try to live life in a clean and tidy manner
 - der raat tak jaagane se or subah der se uthne se tathaa nahaane main laaparvaahee karne se is yoga kaa laabh nahin mil paata
 Panchamahapurush Yoga - In astrology, the special yoga formed from the five main planets is called "pancha-mahapurush" yoga
 - mangal se banane vaala panchmahapurush yoga hota he -"ruchak",- agar yah kundali main ho to aatmavishvaas or saahas kaaphi zyada hota he
 The person is in the field of power
 - budh se banane vaala panchmahapurush yoga he - "bhadra",- yah vyakti ko atyadhik teevr buddhi detaa he, vyakti vyavsaayik kshetron main badi safalataa paata he
 - Panchamahapurusha yoga formed from Jupiter is "swan", - it makes a person religious, knowledgeable and highly respected
 - shukr se banane vaala panchmahapurush yoga he - "malavya" ,- yah vyakti ko sampann , samrudh or bhoga-vilaas se yukt banaata he
 - There is a five-headed yoga called "shash" made from Saturn, - it can reach a person to the highest peak in physical life and in career
 - in yogon main se kisi ek yaa zyada ke hone se vyakti jivan main apaar safalataa, dhan , naam yash paata he- ye yoga tabhi prabhaavshaalee hote hai jab centre yaa trikon main hon, or jin grahon se ban rahaa ho ve grah ast na hon
 - If there are five great men in the horoscope, then one should guard against arrogance and superstition

 The special judge of the Arora Central Bureau of Investigation (CBI) while sentencing Laxman said, "in balancing the double interest of society and the guilty, i am of the opinion that the interest of justice will prevail only if the convict of section nine of the Prevention of Corruption Act Under the sentence of four years rigorous imprisonment for the offense and fined one lakh rupees
 " The court said, "the partner of the crime of corruption is generally our own indifference

 ham kahaan aa gaye hai, jahaan rishwat ke bina koi kaam nahin hota
 " adaalat ne kaha ki yahaan tak ki sahi chizon ko sahi samay par karaane ke liye logon ko paise dene ke liye baadhya kiya jaataa he unhone logon se is tarah ke ravaiye se dur rahane kii apil kii
 Showing no mercy to Laxman, the court said that being the president of a political party, he is expected to have shown his character's tenacity at the time of offering bribe but Laxman did not
 lakshmana ke vakil ne patrakaron se kaha ki vah faisle ke khilaaf dilli ucch nyaayalay main apil karenge
 The case dates back to 2001, when news portal 'tehelka
com' conducted a sting operation and caught Laxman on camera taking a bribe from a journalist
 patrkaar hathiyaar vikreta ke bhesh main tha
 Laxman later resigned as BJP President
 tahalaka ne lakshmana ko rishwat raashi sweekaar karte hue camere main kaid kar liya tha
 Laxman took the bribe in return for a promise to help the Indian army to get a contract to supply thermal imagers to the UK fake company, Messrs West Ind International
 tahalaka ne baad main isse sambandhit sidi jari kar di
 a Delhi court had in May 2011 framed corruption charges against Laxman
 lakshmana ne haalanki, kaha tha ki maamle kii jaanch raajnneeti se prerit thi or nishpaksh nahin thi
 Accusing the Congress of providing funds for this sting operation, Laxman said, "the Congress used Tehelka's tapes in the 2004 general election, which proves that the Congress or the people who were interested in it, Funded the project, which implicated me
 " Targeting the BJP on the pretext of Laxman, Congress spokesperson Rashid Alvi said that this was the first time that a national leader of a national party had been sentenced to rigorous imprisonment

 waite main badhotaree ke baad petrol 57
 59 from 16 rupees

 21 per liter

 dilli main public transport kaa safar aasaan banane ke liye aam aadmi party sarkaar ne somvaar ko 'kaaman mobility card' laanch kar diya
 This card, launched in association with Delhi Metro Rail Corporation (DMRC), will now be known as 'ONE'
 rajghat bas depo main laanchake dauraan parivahan mantri kailash gahalot, parivahan vibhaag or DMRC ke tamaam adhikari maujuud rahe
 The 'common Mobility Card' can be used simultaneously in metro and buses
 nae luk or dizin ke saath laanch hue is card ko 'van dilli' van ride' kaa slogan diya gaya he
 The new 'common Mobility Card' is completely different from the blue color card of Metro, whose design is also different
 isamen dilli sarkaar, metro, ditisi ke logo ke saath-saath charchit imaaraton kii tasviir bhi bani hui he
 All the dtcs and cluster buses of Delhi will have electronic ticketing machines (etms)
 ETM kii madad se pick point se drop point kii jaankaree dekar card ko swip karnaa hoga
 After this, the rental amount will be deducted from the card
 ETM se baqayada ek parchi bhi milegi jisamencard main bakaayaa raashi kii jaankaree hogi
 Apart from metro station, 'common Mobility Card' will be able to be recharged through online
 smart metro card kii tarah nayaa ONE card 100 rupye main kharida ja saktaa he
 Of these 100 rupees, 50 rupees will be taken as security amount
 saath hi nae card ke liye bhi nunatam raashi200 rupye kaa richarge karana hoga
 One card can be purchased from the DTC bus pass counter in addition to the metro station
 iske alaava purana nile rang vaala metro smart card bhi ditisi or cluster bason main 'kaaman mobility card' kii tarah istemaal kiya ja sakegaa
 Transport Minister Kailash Gehlot said that the trial of this card started in February 2018
